### Shared-field × surface policy

A state applies where the field is meaningful to an available output; output and terminal applicability remain in their own matrices. `host-enforced` means the product accepts the canonical field but replaces weaker caller input with a stricter host-owned value. One evidence list per surface grounds the matrix without repeating identical paths in every cell.

| backend:rough | connector | topology | render | lossy | passed | backend-claim-matrix@3/connector/topology/render | path topology remains on the carrier while the visible sketch is a flattened contour projection — The exact authored path remains as an invisible semantic carrier, but arbitrary curves are flattened to typed routed contours for the visible sketch. |
| backend:rough | connector | subpaths | render | emulated | passed | backend-claim-matrix@3/connector/subpaths/render | two typed contours render and hit-test without a synthetic bridge |
| backend:rough | connector | closedness | render | lossy | passed | backend-claim-matrix@3/connector/closedness/render | authored closed carrier retained while visible ribbon is rebuilt from the routed points — Sketch shafts are rebuilt from routed geometry and do not preserve explicit closed-subpath semantics. |
| backend:rough | connector | bend-radius | render | lossy | passed | backend-claim-matrix@3/connector/bend-radius/render | exact rounded carrier retained while the visible sketch uses the declared routed projection — The authored rounded carrier remains exact, but the visible sketch follows its routed polyline and cannot preserve the continuous bend radius. |
| backend:rough | connector | stroke-opacity | render | emulated | passed | backend-claim-matrix@3/connector/stroke-opacity/render | stroke-opacity=0.65 present on the visible generated stroke |
| backend:rough | connector | stroke-cap | render | emulated | passed | backend-claim-matrix@3/connector/stroke-cap/render | stroke-linecap=square present on the visible generated stroke |
| backend:rough | connector | stroke-join | render | emulated | passed | backend-claim-matrix@3/connector/stroke-join/render | stroke-linejoin=miter present on the visible generated stroke |
| backend:rough | connector | stroke-miter | render | emulated | passed | backend-claim-matrix@3/connector/stroke-miter/render | stroke-miterlimit=7 present on the visible generated stroke |
| backend:rough | connector | dash-array | render | emulated | passed | backend-claim-matrix@3/connector/dash-array/render | stroke-dasharray=6 3 present on the visible generated stroke |
| backend:rough | connector | dash-offset | render | emulated | passed | backend-claim-matrix@3/connector/dash-offset/render | stroke-dashoffset=2 present on the visible generated stroke |
| backend:rough | connector | dash-restart | render | lossy | passed | backend-claim-matrix@3/connector/dash-restart/render | 6 generated stroke subpaths restart independently — A rough stroke may contain multiple generated stroke subpaths, so SVG dash restart boundaries can differ. |
| backend:rough | connector | path-length | render | lossy | passed | backend-claim-matrix@3/connector/path-length/render | one pathLength value spans 6 generated stroke subpaths — One pathLength value spans generated stroke subpaths, so a sketch cannot retain one authored path calibration exactly. |
| backend:rough | connector | paint-order | render | emulated | passed | backend-claim-matrix@3/connector/paint-order/render | paint-order=stroke fill present on the visible generated stroke |
| backend:rough | connector | non-scaling-stroke | render | emulated | passed | backend-claim-matrix@3/connector/non-scaling-stroke/render | vector-effect=non-scaling-stroke present on the visible generated stroke |

This matrix covers render outputs only; hosted non-render tools such as `mutate` and `build` remain in the MCP tool registry.

| png | public | direct: renderMermaidPNG / createMermaidBrowserPNGRenderer (native Node/Bun or injected browser rasterizer) | direct: am render (--format png) | unavailable: none — PNG rasterization is a host tool, not a sandbox SDK method | direct: render_png | direct: render_png | direct: Save PNG / Copy PNG (renderMermaidPNGInBrowserWithReceipt) | unavailable: none — The site build copies curated PNG assets but exposes no PNG render adapter | enforced | srgb | not-applicable | output-security@2, output-color-profile@1, png-output-policy@3, render-contract@1 |

### Family executable conformance

A `native` family cell requires both a native descriptor declaration and a passed canonical-example witness. Extensions are staged and rolled back if any native witness fails or changes across the two deterministic runs.

### Family semantic-role / Scene-primitive evidence

Each descriptor declares only its positive role/primitive realizations. The registry expands that authority across all core primitives, so every negative cell is explicit and diagnosed; conformance fixtures exercise the exact positive set.

## Syntax capability ledger

Stable feature IDs are projected from the pinned upstream manifest; stable dimension IDs come from the syntax contract. A native feature state is scoped to its one classified dimension and is not a blanket family-parity claim. Official-document-only constructs remain source-preserved until executable evidence promotes them. CI rejects every missing row and every `absent` state.

### Stable syntax dimensions

| Dimension ID | Label | Contract |
|---|---|---|
| identity-routing | Identity and routing | Family identity, headers, aliases, routing, lifecycle and maturity. |
| document-framing | Document framing | Frontmatter, directives, comments, titles and accessibility framing. |
| grammar | Grammar | Statements, nesting, ordering, delimiters, optional forms and invalid-input behavior. |
| text | Text | Labels, Markdown/HTML/math text, escaping, Unicode, graphemes and multiline behavior. |
| authored-appearance | Authored appearance | Themes, classes, inline styles, link styles and family styling syntax. |
| semantic-identity | Semantic identity | Stable ids, domain entities, relationships, values, source maps and roles. |
| interaction-assets | Interaction and assets | Links, callbacks, tooltips, icons, images, registries and security behavior. |
| configuration | Configuration | Config keys, validation, renderer/layout selection and ineffective-key diagnostics. |
| processing | Processing | Detection, preservation, parsing, serialization, mutation, verification, layout and Scene lowering. |
| outputs | Outputs | SVG, PNG, terminal projections, accessibility, determinism and output security. |
| evidence | Evidence | Official provenance, executable fixtures, divergences and semantic evidence. |

### Family / syntax-dimension classifications
